scales, the implications for our quantum classifier become increasingly significant. While the number of qubits does impose limitations on the size of the ensemble that can be utilized, it does not restrict the volume of data that can be processed. This powerful capability enables the classifier to efficiently handle datasets containing millions of data points and thousands of features. Importantly, the constraints related to ensemble size can be addressed through the implementation of a large-scale version of the classifier. By leveraging an iterative outer-loop approach, the ensemble can be dynamically expanded, enhancing flexibility and overall performance. However, it's worth noting that this feature has not yet been implemented in the current version of the classifier.","className":"group paragraph-el text-text-primary mx-0
